Bryce holds numerous certifications (e.g. OSCP, CISSP, ...), and has spoken at various security conferences (i.e. BlackHat, DerbyCon, BSidesLV, etc...).\n\nOn-demand IT services are being publicized as the new normal, but often times these services are misunderstood and hence misconfigured by engineers which can frequently enable red teams to gain, expand, and persist access within Azure environments.
